Cascadia_earthquake_sources.png  
Cascadia subduction zone
From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia

The area of the Cascadia subduction zone.
Coordinates: 45N 124W The Cascadia subduction zone (also referred to as the Cascadia fault) is a convergent plate boundary that stretches from northern Vancouver Island to northern California. It is a very long sloping subduction zone fault that separates the Juan de Fuca and North America plates.

The denser oceanic plate is subducting beneath the less dense continental plate offshore of British Columbia, Washington and Oregon. The North American Plate moves in a general southwest direction, overriding the oceanic plate. The Cascadia Subduction Zone is where the two plates meet.

Tectonic processes active in the Cascadia subduction zone region include accretion, subduction, deep earthquakes, and active volcanism that has included such notable eruptions as Mount Mazama (Crater Lake) about 7,500 years ago, Mount Meager a" height="115" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2015/07/14/19/2A874F1000000578-0-image-m-74_1436899600067.jpg" width="154"/>

       <div class="article-text wide" id="js-article-text">
        <h1>
         Alicia Silverstone posts video of her chewing baby son's food... before feeding him mouth-to-mouth
         <br/>
        </h1>
        <p class="author-section byline-plain">
         By
         <a class="author" href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Jade+Watkins" rel="nofollow">
          Jade Watkins
         </a>
        </p>
        <p class="byline-section">
         <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-published">
          <span class="article-timestamp-label">
           Published:
          </span>
          13:52 EST, 27 March 2012
         </span>
         |
         <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-updated">
          <span class="article-timestamp-label">
           Updated:
          </span>
          10:44 EST, 28 March 2012
         </span>
        </p>
        <div id="articleIconLinksContainer">
         <ul>
          <li class="share-facebook">
          </li>
          <li class="share-twitter">
          </li>
          <li class="share-pinterest">
          </li>
          <li class="share-gplus">
           <span class="g-interactivepost" data-calltoactionlabel="VIEW" data-calltoactionurl="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-2121233/Alicia-Silverstone-feeding-baby-Bear-mouth-mouth-bird-style-YouTube-video.html" data-clientid="746589970956-e10ciaf67a1id9ggu75ph3ds0sthn7j6.apps.googleusercontent.com" data-contentdeeplinkid="/pages" data-contenturl="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-2121233/Alicia-Silverstone-feeding-baby-Bear-mouth-mouth-bird-style-YouTube-video.html" data-cookiepolicy="single_host_origin" data-prefilltext="Alicia Silverstone posts video of her chewing baby son's food... before feeding him mouth-to-mouth">
            <a>
            </a>
           </span>
          </li>
          <li class="share-email">
           <a class="js-email" data-ajax-refresh-everytime="true" data-modal-id="email-modal-overlay" data-modal-type="email-overlay" data-on-mobile="mailto:?subject=Alicia Silverstone posts video of her chewing baby son's food... before feeding him mouth-to-mouth&amp;body=http://www.dailymail.co.uk/tvshowbiz/article-2121233/Alicia-Silverstone-feeding-baby-Bear-mouth-mouth-bird-style-YouTube-video.html" data-placement="top" data-target="/email-article.html?id=2121233" data-toggle="modal" href="#email" title="Email to a friend">
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="share-icons" id="shareLinkTop">
           <a class="js-sl share-link" href="#socialLinks">
           </a>
           <script type="text/javascript">
            var twitterVia = 'DailyMailCeleb';
          DM.later('bundle', function(){
            DM.has('shareLinkTop', 'shareLinks', {
                    'id': '2121233',
                    'title': 'Alicia Silverstone posts video of her chewing baby son\'s food... before feeding him mouth-to-mouth',

                    'eTwitterStatus': ' http://bit.ly/HfupBF via @' + twitterVia,
                    'articleChannelFollowButton': 'DailyMailCeleb',
                    'isChannel': false,
	        'hideEmail': true,
                    'placement': 'top',
                    'anchor': 'tl'});
          });
           </script>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <a class="comments-count home" href="/tvshowbiz/article-2121233/Alicia-Silverstone-feeding-baby-Bear-mouth-mouth-bird-style-YouTube-video.html#comments">
          <span>
          </span>
          <p class="count-number">
           139
          </p>
          <p class="count-text">
           View
           <br/>
           comments
          </p>
         </a>
         <script>
          DM.later('bundle', function(){
            DMS.Article.init('top');
        });
         </script>
        </div>
        <br/>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          Every mother knows that it can often be difficult to get their child to eat their dinner.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          And it seems that Alicia Silverstone has found a very unusual feeding method when it comes to her son Bear's meal time.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          The 35-year-old actress appears to have taken inspiration from the way birds feed their chicks by chewing up her 10-month-old baby boy's food and then spitting it in his mouth.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          <span style="font-weight: bold;">
           SCROLL DOWN FOR VIDEO...
          </span>
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <div class="artSplitter">
         <img alt="Unusual: Clueless actress Alicia Silverstone has posted a video of her chewing baby son's food before feeding him mouth-to-mouth" class="blkBorder" height="808" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/03/27/article-2121233-125BBCC4000005DC-416_638x808.jpg" width="638"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Unusual: Clueless actress Alicia Silverstone has posted a video of her chewing baby son's food before feeding him mouth-to-mouth
          <br/>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <div class="artSplitter">
         <img alt="Like the birds: Alicia is seen spitting chewed up food into her 10-month-old's mouth" class="blkBorder" height="599" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/03/27/article-2121233-125BBCAF000005DC-188_638x599.jpg" width="638"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Like the birds: Alicia is seen spitting chewed up food into her 10-month-old's mouth
          <br/>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          In a video she posted on her blog, the Clueless actress sits on the couch with Bear during feeding time.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          Holding a small bowl, she puts a spoonful of food in her mouth, chews it up before feeding it to him mouth-to-mouth.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Baby Bear Blu clearly knows the drill, as he eagerly reaches to his mother's lips for a mouthful.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <div class="artSplitter">
         <img alt="Getting it prepared: Alicia chews up her son's food in her mouth" class="blkBorder" height="793" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/03/27/article-2121233-125BBCC0000005DC-690_640x793.jpg" width="640"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Getting it prepared: Alicia chews up her son's food in her mouth
          <br/>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          Alicia explains the process in an accompanied written post on her blog.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          'I just had a delicious breakfast of miso soup, collards and radish steamed and drizzled with flax oil, cast iron mochi with nori wrapped outside, and some grated daikon. Yum!' she wrote.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          'I fed Bear the mochi and a tiny bit of veggies from the soup from my mouth to his.
         </font>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <div class="artSplitter">
         <img alt="Eager: Baby Bear Blu clearly knows the drill, as he eagerly reaches to his mother's lips for a mouthful" class="blkBorder" height="652" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/03/27/article-2121233-125BBCBC000005DC-613_638x652.jpg" width="638"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Eager: Baby Bear Blu clearly knows the drill, as he eagerly reaches to his mother's lips for a mouthful
          <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          </font>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          'Its his favorite...and mine.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          'He
 literally crawls across the room to attack my mouth if Im eating. This
 video was taken about a month or 2 ago when he was a bit wobbly. Now he
 is grabbing my mouth to get the food!'
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          The method of her feeding is similar to the way birds feed their young, aside from the regurgitation process.
         </font>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <div class="artSplitter">
         <img alt="Pleased: Alicia clearly looks pleased with herself following the process" class="blkBorder" height="764" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/03/27/article-2121233-125BBCA3000005DC-930_638x764.jpg" width="638"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Pleased: Alicia clearly looks pleased with herself following the process
          <br/>
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <div class="artSplitter">
         <img alt="Unhygienic? Fox News asked medical and nutritional experts what they thought of the feeding method for humans, with one believing it to be an unhygienic method" class="blkBorder" height="830" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/03/27/article-2121233-125BBC9B000005DC-133_640x830.jpg" width="640"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Unhygienic? Fox News asked medical and nutritional experts what they thought of the feeding method for humans, with one believing it to be an unhygienic method
          <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          </font>
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="floatRHS">
         <img alt="Feeding on the go: Alicia last week breastfed Bear Blu as she went for a stroll with her husband Christopher Jarecki" class="blkBorder" height="611" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2012/03/27/article-2121233-123245E7000005DC-27_308x611.jpg" width="308"/>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Feeding on the go: Alicia last week breastfed Bear Blu as she went for a stroll with her husband Christopher Jarecki
         </p>
        </div>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          Parent birds eat, partially digest the food, then regurgitate it to feed the young.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Fox News asked medical and nutritional experts what they thought of the feeding method for humans.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          'It doesn't seem like a hygienic practice,' one doctor told the site.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Alicia is known to be a staunch vegan and has also set up a sanctuary for rescued pets in Los Angeles.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          Her Baby Bear Blu was born at the beginning of last May, weighing 7lbs 15oz.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em;">
          When he was born, the couple's delighted spokesperson said: 'Mom and Dad are completely in love,' and added that the newborn was 'beautiful'.
          <br/>
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          Silverstone said before his birth that she couldn't wait for her new role as a parent.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          'I've been wanting to have a baby since I was two years old  I'm destined to be a mother,' she said.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          She wed her husband Christopher Jarecki, 40, - the lead singer of group S.T.U.N., radio presenter and a basketball coach - in June 2005 in an idyllic beach-front ceremony in Lake Tahoe, which is on the California-Nevada border.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          After meeting outside a movie theatre in 1997, the couple dated for eight years prior to their marriage.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          Throughout her pregnancy committed animal activist Alicia has been promoting her new book, The Kind Diet, which follows vegan principles.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
         <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
          The actress last appeared in the 2008 film Tropic Thunder but is set to star in upcoming films The Art Of Getting By, Vamps and Butter.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
        <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/01U6VNkGPN8" width="640">
        </iframe>

              <img alt="The Cascadia Earthquake.

Cascadia_earthquake_sources.png  
Cascadia subduction zone
From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia

The area of the Cascadia subduction zone.
Coordinates: 45N 124W The Cascadia subduction zone (also referred to as the Cascadia fault) is a convergent plate boundary that stretches from northern Vancouver Island to northern California. It is a very long sloping subduction zone fault that separates the Juan de Fuca and North America plates.

The denser oceanic plate is subducting beneath the less dense continental plate offshore of British Columbia, Washington and Oregon. The North American Plate moves in a general southwest direction, overriding the oceanic plate. The Cascadia Subduction Zone is where the two plates meet.

Tectonic processes active in the Cascadia subduction zone region include accretion, subduction, deep earthquakes, and active volcanism that has included such notable eruptions as Mount Mazama (Crater Lake) about 7,500 years ago, Mount Meager a" height="115" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2015/07/14/19/2A874F1000000578-0-image-m-74_1436899600067.jpg" width="154"/>

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '&lt;div id="' + id + '"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
            $(node).after(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n});
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=tvshowbiz&amp;pageSize=10',
            total: 17.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
       </script>
      </div>

A sheriff says a 16-year-old girl who survived a small-plane crash and then hiked to safety reported that her step-grandparents died in the accident.

Okanogan County Sheriff Frank Rogers said Tuesday that Autumn Veatch told him Leland and Sharon Bowman of Marion, Montana, died in Saturday's crash. Searchers planned to resume looking for the wreckage early Tuesday.

The girl told Rogers they were flying in the clouds until the sky suddenly opened up to a mountain and they crashed into the trees.

Veatch told authorities she stayed at the crash site for a day before hiking down. A motorist picked her up Monday and drove her 30 miles east to a general store, where employees called 911.

The man held the Italian woman hostage for several minutes as he yelled religious fanaticism at the crowd with police powerless to act. 

One witness said: ?It seemed like a scene from ISIS. He made the girl get down on her knees like you see in the terrorists' videos, while he held a knife to her throat. The only thing missing was the orange jumpsuit.'

Others told Il Messaggero he was yelling 'incomprehensible things, but among them &quot;Allah is great&quot;'.  

Chiara Frisco, from Vasto on the Adriatic coast, who was visiting her sister in Rome to celebrate her graduation, said she feared ?the worst? when the knifeman grabbed her.

Cascadia_earthquake_sources.png  
Cascadia subduction zone
From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia

The area of the Cascadia subduction zone.
Coordinates: 45&deg;N 124&deg;W The Cascadia subduction zone (also referred to as the Cascadia fault) is a convergent plate boundary that stretches from northern Vancouver Island to northern California. It is a very long sloping subduction zone fault that separates the Juan de Fuca and North America plates.

The denser oceanic plate is subducting beneath the less dense continental plate offshore of British Columbia, Washington and Oregon. The North American Plate moves in a general southwest direction, overriding the oceanic plate. The Cascadia Subduction Zone is where the two plates meet.

Tectonic processes active in the Cascadia subduction zone region include accretion, subduction, deep earthquakes, and active volcanism that has included such notable eruptions as Mount Mazama (Crater Lake) about 7,500 years ago, Mount Meager a" width="45" height="43" /&gt;
